				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Heures mystiques, Opp.29-30 (Boëllmann, Léon)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>

</th>
<td>100 pieces
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1895–96
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Vol. 1 (Op.29) contains 5 masses (entrée, offertoire, élévation, communion, sortie), and 27 versets for various uses.<br />
Vol. 2 (Op.30) contains 5 masses (entrée, offertoire, élévation, communion, sortie), and 23 versets for various uses.
</p>
